 Special scheme for Kashmiri farmers launched: Now NAFED will buy apples from farmers
 Farmers of Jammu and Kashmir are expecting double benefit
 Local administration and central government is making all efforts to give national and international market to apple farmers of Jammu and Kashmir
 isi ke tahat guuruuvaar ko rajyapal satyapal malik ne srinagar main seb kisaanon ke liye bazaar hastkshep lakshya yojana (market intervation torget skim) ko laanch kiya
 Under this scheme, apples will be purchased from farmers at remunerative prices through the Central Government's Nodal Procurement Agency or NAFED
 rajyapal ne kaha ki ab kisaan sebon ko bechney se judi dikkaton se khud ko dur rakh paaenge or ve apana puraa dhyaan behatar kism ke seb ke utpaadan par de paaenge

 unhone kaha ki desh ke 75 pratishat sebon kii paidaavaar jammu evam kashmir main hoti he or nayaa tantra is vyapaar ko badhaava degaa, jisase kisaanon kii kamai main jabardast ijapha hoga
 The Governor said that C-grade apples make up 40 per cent of the total yield, at present only three to seven rupees per kg is available to the farmers, but after the implementation of this scheme, its value will be doubled and tripled
 rajyapal ne kaha ki seb market turnover 8000 karod prati varsh he, or isse 7 lakh parivaar pratyaksh or apratyaksh rup se jude hue hai
 He said that more attention needs to be given to this sector
 unhone kaha ki ab NAFED kisaanon se sabon kii kharid karegaa or kisaanon ko har kism ke seb ke liye milane vaali keemten bad jaaegi
 During this, Governor Satyapal Malik also warned people who threaten apple farmers in Kashmir
 rajyapal satyapal malik ne kaha ki aise log jald se jald sudhar jaaen, anyathaa sarkaar unke khilaaf karrwai karegi

 in logon kii shikaayat he ki bhartee prakriya se naaraaz kuch logon ne hycourt main yachika daal di, rajya sarkaar ne is maamle main thik se pairvi nahin kii or nateeja ye hua ki court ne puri prakriya hi roak di or parinaam ghoshit nahin ho paaya

 aise main sarkaar nai bhartee prakriya laai he jo isse alag he or uskaa puraani bhartee vaale maamle se koi lenaa dena nahin he

 magar riselt aata he ek saal baad, 3 farvari 2016 ko

 isi main 2014 se 2016 aa chukaa he
 Those who passed in Mains are subjected to physical examination
 yah pariksha kai charnon main aktubar se lekar 12 disambar 2016 tak puri hoti he

 The noise of campaigning for the sixth phase of the elections to the 16th Assembly of Uttar Pradesh came to a halt at 5 pm on Sunday
 nirvachan ayogke sutron ke mutabik chathe charan ke chunaav main pradesh ke saharanpur, prabuddhanagar, mujffarnagar, meerut, bagpat, gajiabad, panchasheel nagar, gautamabuddha nagar, bulandshahr, aligarh, hathras, mathura tathaa agra samet 13 jilon kii kul 68 vidhansabha siton ke liye aagaamee 28 farvari ko matdaan hoga
 He informed that in the sixth phase, more than two crore 14 lakh voters, including 95 lakh 19 thousand women, will be able to decide the fate of a total of 1103 candidates
 matdaan ke liye 22137 matdaan kendra banaaye gayi hai jin par 30028electranik voting mashin(iviem) belatting ikaiyaan istemaal kii jaaengi
 Sources said that sufficient number of Central Paramilitary Force and PAC personnel have been deployed to conduct the polling in an independent, fair and fear-free manner
 unhone bataaya ki ayog ne sambandhit jilon ke prashasan se kaha he ki ve yah sunishchit karen ki prachaar kaary samaapt hone ke baad ve rajaneta, kaaryakarta tathaa prachaarak jo vidhansabha kshetra se baahar ke hai or jo nirvachan kshetra ke matadaata nahin hai, ilaake se baahar chale jaaen
 The Congress, BJP, SP and BSP exerted their full strength in the campaign of campaigning in the sixth phase, especially in the electoral battle of the region, which is considered as an area with farmer-based politics
 congress ke liye pramukh rup se party adhyaksh sonia gandhi, dal ke mahasachiv rahul gandhi, digvijay singh, kendriya mantri salmaan khurshid, benny prasad verma tathaa shriprakash jaiswal ne prachaar kiya
 The Rashtriya Lok Dal (RLD), along with its ally Congress, campaigned vigorously
 bhaajapa ke liye mukhya rup se iske rashtriya adhyaksh nitin gadakari, varisht netaa laalkrishna adwani, loksabhaa main vipaksh kii netaa sushamaa swaraj, party upaadhyaksh calraj mishra, purv rashtriya adhyaksh rajnath singh tathaa rajyasabha main netaa pratipaksh arun jetali ne tufaani daure kiye
 Party president and state chief minister Mayawati, his close aides Satish Chandra Mishra and Nasimuddin Siddiqui campaigned mainly for the ruling BSP
 vidhansabha chunaav ke chathe charan main pashchimi uttar pradesh main prabhaav rakhane vaale rashtriya lokdal (ralod) ke garh kahe jane vaale ilaake main chunaav honge jisamen ralod ke ‘yuvaraj’ jayant choudhary, pradesh sarkaar ke prabhaavshaalee mantri ramvir upaadhyaay tathaa jaiveer singh, rajya vidhanmandal main bhaajapa ke upanetaa hukum singh tathaa purv mukhyamantri kalyaan singh ke bete rajvir singh samet kai pramukh siyaasi hastiyon kii chunavi kismat kaa faisla hoga
 Rashid Masood, the 'muslim face' who took the Congress's hand and left the SP, will also be in the election phase of the sixth phase
 unke bhattije imran masood saharanpur kii nakud seat se chunaav lard rahe hai
 The Jugalbandi of SP and Shahi Imam of Delhi's Jama Masjid, Maulana Ahmed Bukhari, will be gauged by the trend of the Beht seat of Saharanpur, where Bukhari's son-in-law Omar Ali is contesting from the SP ticket
 charchit vidhayak haji yaqub kuraishi is baar ralod ke tikat par meerut kii saradhana seat se chunaav lard rahe hai
 His constituency will also vote in the sixth phase
